    "use strict";

    if($('.glb-grid-24')){

        var cardId = '#ge-card-classificacao-c857540d-9ed7-4a9d-a866-4343fbe2504f',
                classificacaoFeedReady = false,
                classificacaoCardReady = false;

            $(document).on('bastian-feed-card_rendered', cardId, function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Feed Ready');
                classificacaoFeedReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

            $(document).on('card-classificacao-ready', function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Card Ready');
                classificacaoCardReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

        var initCardClassificacao = function(){
            if(classificacaoCardReady && classificacaoFeedReady){
                $('#ge-card-classificacao-c857540d-9ed7-4a9d-a866-4343fbe2504f').show();
            }
        }
    }

    try {

      var classificacao = new CardClassificacao({
        context: '#ge-card-classificacao-c857540d-9ed7-4a9d-a866-4343fbe2504f'
      });

      var classificacaoTracking = new CardClassificacaoTracking("c857540d-9ed7-4a9d-a866-4343fbe2504f");

    } catch (err) {}

});
